    <li> No blending brush which I knew beforehand but it&#x27;s a bummer.&lt;br /&gt;They smell at first so wash them! I used baby shampoo.&lt;br /&gt;Four of the brushes come with protective covers (I wish and thought all did) but that&#x27;s really nice for cleaning them because they are supposed to be dried upside down.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;How I clean:&lt;br /&gt;I know there&#x27;s a lot of fancy brush cleaning products but I&#x27;ve done it two different home remedy ways.&lt;br /&gt;first way:&lt;br /&gt;Get a small plate and poor some Johnsons Baby shampoo into it then get your brush wet and swirl it around.  If the brushes are new, it&#x27;s harder to tell when they&#x27;re clean because no makeup will be coming out, so just use your best judgement; if they are old but just need to be cleaned, swirl them in the shampoo until the makeup stops making the soap brown (blue green ext.). Then paint circles on your hand as you rinse wish warm water so make sure each hair gets the shampoo off.&lt;br /&gt;Second way:&lt;br /&gt;I do the same as the first but instead of using Baby shampoo I use a mixture of dish soap and virgin olive oil, the dish soap is harsh on the brushes so use the oil to condition them.&lt;br /&gt;To dry:&lt;br /&gt;You never want to dry your brushes hair up.  Because any water residue will drip down into the brush and loosen the glue holding the hairs.  So that is when brush covers come in handy there is a product called the Brush Guard that you can buy separately that will protect your brushes.  I just tape them upside down to my mirror and let them dry that way!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Hope my novel helps at least one person! :P</li>

    <li> This is one of those classic cases of, \\&quot;You can&#x27;t judge a book by its cover.\\&quot; I have good things, as well as bad things to say about this purchase, but overall, I am pleased and happy with what I purchased at the price of which I paid.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;PROS: Obviously I am going to start out with the good things about this product!&lt;br /&gt;- Sleek appearance. I recently spent much more on a set of \\&quot;professional\\&quot; brushes and was very disappointed at how stiff the bristles were. I actually ended up RETURNING them, and I rarely return make up products.&lt;br /&gt;- Easy to store. With the carrying pouch allowing you to roll up the brushes, it makes it super easy to keep them organized.&lt;br /&gt;- Shipped with extra protection. When I opened this product, I found that the pouch was tightly rolled up, tied, and placed in a cellophane wrapper. When I unrolled the pouch, I found that each brush was wrapped in cellophane separately, and the face brushes actually come with hard plastic protectors to keep on at all times. I really thought this was great, since the larger brushes can so easily become mis-shaped.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;CONS: Cause every review has to have em right?&lt;br /&gt;- SMELL. The smell when you take this out of it&#x27;s box will literally almost knock you over. It is terrible! This is where my comment, \\&quot;You can&#x27;t judge a book by its cover,\\&quot; or by its smell in this case. Seriously, prepare yourself!&lt;br /&gt;- The pouch itself. The pouch was a huge let down in my opinion. However, I did not buy this product for the case. So if you are buying this because you really want a carrying case, don&#x27;t buy this product. The seems were sewn together VERY sloppy, and some of the sections that divide the brushes appeared to not have been sewn shut at all! Very disappointing in this aspect.&lt;br /&gt;- There is an extremely weird powder on these brushes when you open them. If you read the product description very closely, it says to be SURE to wash these brushes before your first use. THIS IS EXTREMELY IMPORTANT!!!!!!!!!!!!!! If you don&#x27;t read anything else in this review, which you really should because I KNOW my make up products, make SURE you read this. When I took the brushes out of the cellophane wrappers and ran my fingers through the bristles, this weird, gross smelling powder went flying into the air. Now, I am giving this company the benefit of the doubt by assuming this powder was something that settled in these bristles upon shipment.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;OVERALL, I really do like this product and for the price, I am very happy I bought it. BUT you NEED to make sure you wash these before you use them. Trust me, you do NOT want that smelly, gross stuff on your face. DO NOT WASH THESE BRUSHES WITH YOUR SHAMPOO OR DISH SOAP! These products are WAY too harsh, and they will strip your bristles. However, I am in no way saying you need to go spend $15.00 on \\&quot;special brush soap.\\&quot; I use and have always used baby shampoo on my brushes, even my expensive ones. It works great and easily washes out. Also, make sure you re-shape your brushes once you have them washed and that you let them COMPLETELY dry before you try and use them.</li>

    <li> I really wanted to love these brushes and out of the box I did. These are completely gorgeous brushes and by FAR the most beautiful $13 brushes you will ever see. Out of the box I was in love. They are a hot pink reddish color with a matching case. The handles are long and sleek and so smooth and silky to the touch. The case is beautiful, sleek, heavy duty, and there was NO stitching coming undone. They look very professional. Also, there was only a faint smell coming from these brushes and I have had more expensive brushes that smell much MUCH worse. It seems SHANY took peoples suggestions with the smell and the case as I had no issues with either. So looks get 5 stars here.    This is primarily an eye brush kit. To my knowledge all these brushes are natural hair (appear to be pony, not including the eyebrow comb). It is rare to find natural hair brushes at this low of a price, this is NOT to say synthetic brushes are cheaper, synthetic brushes can be outstanding and far better than natural and in this case these are really low quality natural hairs.    The hairs, especially of the larger brushes feel like straw against my face. They are really not soft and silky. These brushes very thin and not very dense, which is expected at this price but I mean the brushes really fall flat against your face. The fan brush is so so thin it is unusable. But this isn&#x27;t the main problem.    The main problem is shedding. The first time you wash brushes it is common for loose hairs to come out but after that shedding should stop. These brushes shed SO much during the first wash, both the large and small brushes and there was hair all over my counter and my hands. Also there was a strange black powder coming out of some of the brushes... I am also careful to not get water in the ferrule so this should not have happened. Also when washing my brushes the smaller sized powder/blush brush handle came right off. There is very little glue used to hold the handle on and to hold the hairs inplace which is a huge problem. I was able to easily krazy glue the handle back into place but still not a good first impression. I put these brushes in my brush tree (hanging upside down) and let them dry overnight and the glue set. My big mistake here was not using a brush guard, you MUST use a mesh BRUSH GUARD when on the two larger brushes in this set (made by coastal scents available here on amazon, buy the muti pack). I reshaped the brushes while they were wet in my hand but that wasn&#x27;t enough and they dried deformed.    I washed these brushes a second time before using (which I don&#x27;t normally do) and they still shed (not as much thankfully) making me very weary to use on myself. Also I was using baby shampoo which I use on all my brushes as it is very gentle and nurturing to the hair, especially natural. Do not I repeat DO NOT use dish soap or vinegar or any chemical like that, they will strip the natural hair and make these brushes weaker and scratchier than they already are.    Above all there are much much better brushes in this price range, real techniques makes an eye and face kit each about the price of these that absolutely tower over the quality of these. Eco tools also makes better brushes than these. Coastal scents also have a natural and synthetic 22 piece brush mix that is much better than these. All these brush kits are available shipped and sold by amazon.     <li> For most of my life, I did not have the money or was not willing to spend the money to invest in expensive makeup brushes. I used the sponge-tip applicators that came with eye shadow to apply it and owned a VERY cheap, small set of blush/eye/lip brushes that I used for many years.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In the last few years, I got back into makeup as a hobby and decided to get some new brushes. I thought the price of this collection of SHANY Professional brushes was super reasonable for all you get. Not only do you get 12 brushes, but you get a pouch that can store/carry them in. The pouch has individual pockets for each brush and each brush comes with a protective sleeve. The smaller ones have a long flimsy cellophane-type sleeve but the bigger brushes have have a heavier plastic protector for the brush tip that could be used to reshape the brush after washing.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The kit includes:&lt;br /&gt;1.  Detail shadow brush&lt;br /&gt;2.  Lip gloss brush&lt;br /&gt;3.  Angled eye liner brush&lt;br /&gt;4.  Small shadow brush&lt;br /&gt;5.  Extra-large shadow brush&lt;br /&gt;6.  Face powder brush&lt;br /&gt;7.  Fan brush&lt;br /&gt;8.  Blush brush&lt;br /&gt;9  Large shadow brush&lt;br /&gt;10. Smudging sponge (sponge-tip shadow applicator/blender)&lt;br /&gt;11. Lash/Brow brush&lt;br /&gt;12. Eye liner brush&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I was a bit surprised at the exclusion of a contour brush and a lip liner brush. Both the #3 and #12 liner brushes specify (in the description) that they are intended for eyes and nothing in the description addressed contouring.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;My favorite and most-used of this set are 4, 5, 9 an 10. I use the 5 or 9 to blend all my eye shadow together to soften down the darker crease color for daytime and blend the colors together. I use 10 as a shadow applicator not as a smudging tool. I stopped using 6 and 8 due to the hair dropping (see more on this below). I now use RealTechniques brushes (the Expert Face Brush and the Stippling Brush) for powder and blush and have yet to see either drop a single hair. There are some brushes, like 3, 11 and 12, that I have never used because I don&#x27;t use liquid eye liner, already had a brow brush I liked better, etc.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;According to the pamphlet in the box, these brushes are made of goat and badger hair. They are quite soft. Most of the brush tips are medium to chestnut brown. The handles are a pretty Chinese lacquer-type red and the ferrules are glossy black. The brushes are not labelled with their name (i.e., \\&quot;Blush brush\\&quot;) but are labelled with a number, so as long as you keep the enclosed pamphlet, you&#x27;ll be able to keep straight which brush is for what use. Note that there are multiple sets of these SHANY brushes. This set has brown hair brushes and comes in a red pouch. There is another set that comes in a purple pouch and has, I believe, black hair brushes.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Quality-wise, it is a mixed bag. I have yet to see the ferrule of one of these brushes come apart from the handle, which is something I saw happen with my older cheap brush set. On the other hand, while I have not noticed the eye brushes dropping hairs much, I have seen a LOT of dropped hairs from the larger (blush and powder) brushes. I was regularly finding hairs on my face. As noted above, I stopped using the blush and powder brushes of this set because of the frequency of dropped hairs and now use RealTechniques brushes for that.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The pouch these brushes come in is red and the material used (some sort of plastic) feels very cheap. It is bulky enough (even without the brushes in it) that I can&#x27;t imagine ever using it to travel with because I have no need to carry that many brushes with me, but some may find it very useful for travel/storage.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I think this would be a fine starter kit (and a nice present) for a young lady just starting out wearing makeup or newly out on her own. It would also be a nice kit for someone of any age who did not have the money (or want to spend the money) on the more expensive brushes.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Frankly, if I had known about RealTechniques brushes BEFORE ordering this SHANY Professional set, I probably would not have purchased this set. I find the RealTechniques brushes to be of higher quality (but still reasonably priced) and, unlike these SHANY brushes which are made of animal hair, RT brushes are cruelty free.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;4.0 stars for the bargain price given the size of the collection.&lt;br /&gt;3.25 stars for the quality of the brushes (hair dropping, animal hair).&lt;br /&gt;2.5 stars for the quality of the pouch.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Average: 3 1/4 starsechniques brushes BEFORE ordering this SHANY Professional set, I probably would not have purchased this set. I find the RealTechniques brushes to be of higher quality (but still reasonably priced) and, unlike these SHANY brushes which are made of animal hair, RT brushes are cruelty free.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;4.0 stars for the bargain price given the size of the collection.&lt;br /&gt;3.25 stars for the quality of the brushes (hair dropping, animal hair).&lt;br /&gt;2.5 stars for the quality of the pouch.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Average: 3 1/4 stars</li>
